msg:Jiujiang Yuanzhou International Hotel, originated in the 1980s, the building is relatively old, the decoration style is standard, grand and exemplary.
1. I travel all over the country, choose hotels for comprehensive reference, and then make a decisive decision. After checking in, the ideal degree is roughly 80%.
2. I am a high-level member of Ctrip, and the price Ctrip gives me is a very favorable price.
3. Choose a five-star hotel. If the building is built in the 1980s and 1990s, it is relatively solid, the room decoration is grand and heavy, the lobby is wide and majestic, and the disadvantage is that some are a bit old. I personally think that if you pay attention to details and maintain it, you can keep it clean and tidy, and there is no damage in the room, it still looks classic and high-end.
4. Yuanzhou International Hotel has first-class service, the waiter is dignified and generous, and the words and expressions are focused and elegant everywhere, so that guests can feel very respected.
5. The front desk clerk took the initiative to upgrade me to a room facing Nanhu. The room is bright, the carpet is clean, the bed is soft, and lying down is deeply sunken in the bedding, the whole body fits, and the sleep is deep.
6. The room attendant spoke softly and delivered fruits. There was a bed-making service before going to bed. I asked the room attendant how to eat dinner in the hotel. She was very enthusiastic and polite and led me to the restaurant.
7. The dishes in Nanguo Restaurant are delicious, and the dishes give people a healthy and tasty feeling.
8. The breakfast is exquisite and complete. Many waiters serve guests, and the breakfast coupons can be used for lunch. This is a very generous move for the hotel to treat guests!
9. The car was parked behind the hotel. When you come out, you need to call the front desk to confirm before opening the door. This needs to be improved.
10. Thank you very much to Yuanzhou International Hotel for giving me a pleasant experience of a night's journey. I will definitely stay at Yuanzhou International again when I come to Jiujiang next time.
